        //set your publishable key
        Stripe.setPublishableKey("pk_live_nlylASNk7bwYCsxbckZuhwZO");

        //callback to handle the response from stripe
        function stripeResponseHandler(status, response) {
            if (response.error) {
                //enable the submit button
                // $("#submit-btn").show();
                 $("#submit-btn").val('Proceed with Purchase');
                  $("#submit-btn").attr('disabled', false);
                // $( "#loader" ).css("display", "none");
                //display the errors on the form
                $("#error-message").html(response.error.message).show();
            } else {
                //get token id
                var token = response['id'];
                //insert the token into the form
                $("#email-form").append("<input type='hidden' name='token' value='" + token + "' />");
                //submit form to the server
                var fields_certs = [];
                var certs = [];
                if($('#UI-Design').is(':checked')) {
                    fields_certs.push('Regular Updates');
                    certs.push('Regular Updates');
                }
                if($('#UI-Development').is(':checked')) {
                    fields_certs.push('Legal Mitigation');
                    certs.push('Legal Mitigation');
                }
                if($('#Marketing-Site').is(':checked')){
                    fields_certs.push('Corporate Preparedness');  
                    certs.push('Corporate Preparedness');
                } 
                if($('#General').is(':checked')) {
                    fields_certs.push('Certificate Recognition');
                    certs.push('Certificate Recognition');
                }


                $.ajax({
                    method: "POST",
                    url: "dev/charge.php",
                    data: {
                        username: $('#Username').val(),
                        password: $('#Password').val(),
                        fname: $('#First-Name').val(),
                        lname: $('#Last-Name').val(),
                        email:$('#Email-Address').val(),
                        couponcode: $('#couponcode').val(),
                        phone: $('#Phone-Number').val(),
                        comp: $('#Company').val(),
                        job: $('#Job-Title').val(),
                        fields_certs: fields_certs.join(", "),
                        certs: certs.join(", "),
                        cardname: $('#range_03').val(),
                        cardnumber:$('#range_04').val(),
                        month:$('#range_06').val(),
                        year:$('#range_07').val(),
                        cvc: $('#range_05').val(),
                        amount: amount,
                        token: token,
                        time:time,
                        subscription_plan:$('input[name=subscription_plan]:checked').val()
                    }
                })
    .done(function( msg ) {
        if(msg!=""){
            window.location.href="https://checkout.coronavirustraining.org/thank-you.html"
        }   
    });
    $("#email-form").submit();
}
}

function stripePay(e) {
    e.preventDefault();
    var valid = cardValidation();

    if(valid) {
        $("#error_show").hide();

        // $("#submit-btn").hide();
        $("#submit-btn").val('Processing');
                  $("#submit-btn").attr('disabled', true);
        $( "#loader" ).css("display", "inline-block");
        Stripe.createToken({
            number: $('#range_04').val(),
            cvc: $('#range_05').val(),
            exp_month: $('#range_06').val(),
            exp_year: $('#range_07').val()
        }, stripeResponseHandler);
                    //submit from callback
                    return false;
                }
            }

function cardValidation () {
    var valid = true;
    if($('#zipcode').val().trim() == ""){
        valid = false;
	    msg="Zip is required";
	    $(".error_show").html(msg).show();
	    return valid;
    }
	if($('#Shared-Equity-Models').is(':checked')) {
	    valid = true;
	}else{
	    valid = false;
	    msg="Please accept Terms & Condition";
	    $(".error_show").html(msg).show();
	    return valid;
	}

   if ($('.content .inner').length) {
        valid = true;
    }else{
        msg="Please read Terms & Condition";
        $(".error_show").html(msg).show();
        valid = false;
        return valid;
    }

    // if ($("input[name='subscription_plan']").is(':checked')){
    //     valid = true;
    // }
    // else {
    //     msg="Please select payment plan";
    //     $(".error_show").html(msg).show();
    //     valid = false;
    //     return valid;
    // }
       
    return valid;
}

    function validateEmail(email) {
        var filter = /^([\w-\.]+)@((\[[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\.)|(([\w-]+\.)+))([a-zA-Z]{2,4}|[0-9]{1,3})(\]?)$/;
        if (filter.test(email)) {
            return true;
        }
        else {
            return false;
        }
    }


    $('#couponcodebtn').click(function(){
        var btn = $(this);
        var couponname = $('#couponcode').val();
        $.ajax({
            method: "POST",
            url: "dev/coupon.php",
            data: {
                coupon: $('#couponcode').val(),
                email:$('#Email-Address').val(),
            },
            success:function(response){
                var obj = $.parseJSON(response);
                if(obj.msg=="success"){

                	if(couponname=="WMTCGHR2019"){
                		 sp1="";
                	}
                	else if(couponname=="THANKSGIVEN50"){
                	    obj.amount = 750;
                	    sp1 = 0;
                	}
                	else{
                		var sp1 = $('input[name="subscription_plan"]:checked').val();

	                    if($(sp1 != null )){
	                        if(sp1==1){
	                            sp1 = 150.00;
	                        }else if(sp1==2){
	                            sp1 = 22.00;
	                        }else{
	                            sp1="";
	                        }
	                    }
                	}
                    

                $('#couponrow').show();
                amount=99-obj.amount+sp1;
                if(parseFloat(amount)<=0) amount = 0;
                $('#coupontext').text("- "+obj.amount.toLocaleString('en-US', { style: 'currency', currency: 'USD' })+" USD");
                $('#copprice').val(obj.amount);           
                btn.text("Valid Coupon");
                $('#aftercoupon').text(parseFloat(amount).toLocaleString('en-US', { style: 'currency', currency: 'USD' })+" USD");
            }else{
                    btn.text("Invalid Code");
                }
            }
        })
    })

    jQuery(document).ready(function(){
        jQuery('.scrollbar-inner').scrollbar({
            "onScroll": function(y, x){
            if((y.scroll!=0) && (y.maxScroll!=0) && y.scroll > y.maxScroll-1000){
                jQuery(".demo").addClass('inner');
                $('#Shared-Equity-Models').attr('disabled',false);
                $('.checkbox-wrapper.checkbox-square.w-checkbox').css('background','rgba(225, 228, 233, .25)');

                // alert(111);
            }else{

            }
        }
        });
        $('input[name="subscription_plan"]').click(function(){
            var sp = $('input[name="subscription_plan"]:checked').val();

            var couponname = $('#couponcode').val();
			if(couponname=="WMTCGHR2019"){
				 sp="";
			}else{
			        if(sp==1){
		                sp = 150.00;
		            }else if(sp==2){
		                sp = 22.00;
		            }
			}
            
            var copprice = $('#copprice').val();    
            amount = 99-copprice +sp;
            $('#coupontext2').text(sp.toLocaleString('en-US', { style: 'currency', currency: 'USD' })+" USD");
            $('#couponrow2').show();
            $('#aftercoupon').text(parseFloat(amount).toLocaleString('en-US', { style: 'currency', currency: 'USD' })+" USD");
            
        });
    }); 
</script>
<script>
var utm_m = utm_s = utm_c = "";
function getUrlParameter(sParam) {
    var sPageURL = window.location.search.substring(1),
        sURLVariables = sPageURL.split('&'),
        sParameterName,
        i;

    for (i = 0; i < sURLVariables.length; i++) {
        sParameterName = sURLVariables[i].split('=');

        if (sParameterName[0] === sParam) {
            return sParameterName[1] === undefined ? true : decodeURIComponent(sParameterName[1]);
        }
    }
};
